ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
Lparameters pKey as Character, pTip as Character, pInc as Integer, pFil as Logical, pRst as Character
Private pTop, pChv

If Empty(pKey) Or Empty(pTip) Or Not InList(pTip, [CPROS], [DPROS])
	=Messagebox('Os ParŌmetros Passados NŃo SŃo Vßlidos...', 0+48, 'Erro!')
	Return .f.
EndIf

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = ThisForm.Caption
ThisForm.cntSombra.lblTitulo.Caption = ThisForm.Caption

If (Alltrim(pKey) = [.])
	pKey = []
EndIf

This.FiltroP 	= Iif(Vartype(pFil) = 'L', '', pFil + ' ')
This.Incremento = Iif(Type('pInc')='N', pInc, 100)
This.TopAtual 	= This.Incremento
This.Campo		= pTip
This.Ordem 		= Iif(pTip=[DESCRICAO], [DPROS], Iif(pTip=[GRUPO], [CGRUS], [CPROS]))
This.plRelease  = .f.
This.Registro   = 0
This.ProcuraI   = Alltrim(pKey) + Replicate([ ], Iif(InList(pTip, [CPROS], [DPROS], [CGRU]), 60, 9) - Len(Alltrim(pKey)))
This.ProcuraF   = Alltrim(pKey) + Replicate(Chr(254), Iif(InList(pTip, [CPROS], [DPROS], [CGRU]), 60, 9) - Len(Alltrim(pKey)))
This.Status     = []
This.Restrito   = [] && Richard Em 02/09/2015 - Incluir Restriń§es Por MovimentańŃo

pTop = This.TopAtual

With ThisForm
	.poDataMgr = CreateObject('fSqlConector', ThisForm.Name)

	If (.poDataMgr.pnIdconn > 0)
		lcQryProd = [Select a.cpros, a.dpros, a.cgrus, a.sGrus, a.codfinp, a.codacbs, a.cclass, a.reffs, a.ifors, a.codcors, a.tamhs, a.tamls, a.tamps, a.dpro2s ] + ;
					[From SigCdPro a ] + ;
					[Where a.] + This.Campo + [ BetWeen '] + This.ProcuraI + [' And '] + This.ProcuraF + [' ] + This.filtroP + ;
					[Order By a.] + This.Ordem

		* Richard Em 02/09/2015 - Incluir Restriń§es Por MovimentańŃo
		If (Type([pRst])=[C]) And Not Empty(pRst)
			If Not fAbrirTabs(.poDataMgr, [SigCdRpo], [LocalRopt], [Dopps = '] + pRst + ['])
				Return .f.
			EndIf
			This.Restrito = Iif(Reccount([LocalRopt]) > 0, pRst, [])
			Use In LocalRopt
			* mena - 18/09/2015 - incluido group by para eliminar linhas repetidas
			lcQryProd = [Select a.Cpros, a.Dpros, a.Cgrus, a.SGrus, a.CodFinp, a.Codacbs, a.Cclass, ] + ;
							   [a.Reffs, a.Ifors, a.CodCors, a.Tamhs, a.Tamls, a.Tamps, a.Dpro2s, a.PesoMs ] + ;
						[From SigCdPro a ] + ;
			    			   Iif(Empty(This.Restrito), [], [Inner Join SigCdRpo b On (a.Cgrus = b.Cgrus Or a.Mercs = b.Mercs) And b.Dopps = '] + This.Restrito + [' ]) + ;
						[Where a.] + This.Campo + [ BetWeen '] + This.ProcuraI + [' And '] + This.ProcuraF + [' ] + This.filtroP + ;
						[group by a.Cpros, a.Dpros, a.Cgrus, a.SGrus, a.CodFinp, a.Codacbs, a.Cclass, ] + ;
						[a.Reffs, a.Ifors, a.CodCors, a.Tamhs, a.Tamls, a.Tamps, a.Dpro2s, a.PesoMs ] + ;
						[Order By a.] + This.Ordem
		EndIf

		With .poDataMgr
			.AddCursor('SigCdPro', 'cPros', 'crProd', '', '', lcQryProd)
		EndWith

		If Not Used('crProd')
			=Messagebox('NŃo foi PossĒvel Criar o Cursor de Produtos...', 0+48, 'Init - crProd')
			Return .f.
		EndIf
		
		This.plAchouRegistro = .f.

		=DoDefault()
	Else
		=Messagebox('ImpossĒvel Efetuar ConexŃo Com o Servidor de Banco de Dados...', 0+48, 'CreateObject')
		Return .f.
	EndIf
EndWith

This.cArquivo = Sys(2023) + [\] + 'Fig' + Sys(2015) + [.jpg]	&& cria arquivo para mostrar foto do produto

This.SqlDados

This.CriaFiltro()
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Destroy
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Destroy
If Not This.plRelease
	This.poDataMgr.Release
EndIf

=DoDefault()
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Activate
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Activate
=DoDefault()
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: frmprod.getCClas
* Classe: fwget (Base: textbox)
* Registro: 163
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista, loQuery, cheFil

SELECT localCls
cheFil = [ cods in (']
scan
	cheFil = cheFil +ALLTRIM(cclass)+ [',']
endscan
chefil = SUBSTR(chefil, 1, LEN(chefil)-2) + [) ]


lcQuery = [Select cods, descs From SigCdCls where ] + cheFil
IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal])) >0

	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		Select crLocal
		Index On cods tag cods
		If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 3), [crLocal], [cods])
			loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crLocal], [cods], This.Value, [SeleńŃo], .t.)
			loLista.mAddColuna('cods',    '', 'C¾digo')
			loLista.mAddColuna('descs', '', 'DescrińŃo')
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf

		If Lastkey() <> 27
			This.Parent.getCClas.Value = CrLocal.Cods
			This.Parent.getDClas.Value = CrLocal.Descs
		Else
			This.Parent.getcClas.Value = ''
			This.Parent.getdClas.Value = ''	
		EndIf

	Else
		This.Parent.getcClas.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.getdClas.Value = ''
	EndIf
ENDIF

This.Parent.getcClas.Refresh
This.Parent.getdClas.Refresh
* Fim ****************************************************************************
ENDPROC

PROCEDURE btnOK.Click
With This.Parent.Parent
	.cpros   = crProd.cpros
	.dpros   = crProd.dpros
	.cgrus   = crProd.cgrus

	If Not Eof('crProd')
		.plAchouRegistro = .t.
	EndIf
	
	.Hide
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

With This.Parent.Parent
	.cpros   = Space(Len(crProd.cpros))
	.dpros   = Space(Len(crProd.dpros))
	.cgrus   = Space(Len(crProd.cgrus))

	.Hide
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

* PROCEDURE Valid
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Valid
Local loLista, loQuery, cheFil, lcGru

SELECT localGrp
cheFil = [ cgrus in (']
scan
	cheFil = cheFil + cgrus + [',']
endscan
chefil = SUBSTR(chefil, 1, LEN(chefil)-2) + [) ]


lcQuery = [Select cgrus, dgrus From SigCdGrp where ] + cheFil
IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal])) >0

	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		Select crLocal
		Index On cgrus tag cgrus
		If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 3), [crLocal], [cgrus])
			loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crLocal], [cgrus], This.Value, [SeleńŃo], .t.)
			loLista.mAddColuna('cgrus',    '', 'C¾digo')
			loLista.mAddColuna('dgrus', '', 'DescrińŃo')
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf

		If Lastkey() <> 27
			This.Parent.getCGru.Value = CrLocal.cgrus
			This.Parent.getDGru.Value = CrLocal.dgrus
		Else
			This.Parent.getcgru.Value = ''
			This.Parent.getdgru.Value = ''	
		EndIf

	Else
		This.Parent.getcgru.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.getdgru.Value = ''
	EndIf
ENDIF

**** Habilita ou desabilita subgrupo
lcgru=this.Value
lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdPsg where cgrus = '] + ALLTRIM(lcgru) + [']
lnRet=(ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal]))
IF RECCOUNT('crLocal') = 0
	thisform.getCSGru.Enabled = .f.
	thisform.getDSGru.Enabled = .f.
	thisform.btnProcSGru.Enabled = .f.
	thisform.btnExclSGru.Enabled = .f.
ELSE
	thisform.getCSGru.Enabled = .T.
	thisform.getDSGru.Enabled = .T.
	thisform.btnProcSGru.Enabled = .T.
	thisform.btnExclSGru.Enabled = .T.
ENDIF

This.Parent.getcGru.Refresh
This.Parent.getdGru.Refresh
This.Parent.getcSGru.Refresh
This.Parent.getdSGru.Refresh

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE Valid

cheFil = [ codigos in (']
scan
	cheFil = cheFil + sgrus + [',']
endscan
chefil = SUBSTR(chefil, 1, LEN(chefil)-2) + [) ]

lcQuery = [Select * From SigCdPsg where cgrus = '] + ALLTRIM(lcgru) + [']

lcQuery = [Select codigos, descricaos From SigCdPsg where cgrus = '] + ALLTRIM(lcgru) + [' and ] + cheFil
IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal])) >0

	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		Select crLocal
		Index On codigos tag codigos
		If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 6), [crLocal], [codigos])
			loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crLocal], [codigos], This.Value, [Sub Grupos], .t.)
			loLista.mAddColuna('Codigos',    '', 'C¾digo')
			loLista.mAddColuna('Descricaos', '', 'DescrińŃo')
			loLista.Show()
		EndIf

		If Lastkey() <> 27
			This.Value = crLocal.codigos
			This.Parent.getDSgru.Value = CrLocal.Descricaos
		Else
			This.Value = ''
			This.Parent.getDSgru.Value = ''
		EndIf
	else
		This.Value = ''
		This.Parent.getDSgru.Value = ''
	EndIf
ELSE

ENDIF
This.Parent.getCSgru.Refresh
This.Parent.getDSgru.Refresh

* Fim ****************************************************************************
ENDPROC

scan
	cheFil = cheFil + codcors + [',']
endscan
chefil = SUBSTR(chefil, 1, LEN(chefil)-2) + [) ]

lcQuery = [Select cods, descs From SigCdCor where ] + cheFil
IF (ThisForm.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [crLocal])) >0
	If Not Empty(This.Value)
		Select crLocal
		Index On Descs tag Descs
		If Not Seek(Padr(This.Value, 40), [crLocal], [Descs])
			loLista = CreateObject([fwBuscaInt], [crLocal], [descs], This.Value, [SeleńŃo], .t.)
			loLista.mAddColuna('descs', '', 'DescrińŃo')
			loLista.mAddColuna('cods',  '', 'C¾digo')

		If Lastkey() <> 27

			This.Parent.getCor.Value = CrLocal.Cods
		Else
			This.Value = ''
			This.Parent.getCor.Value = []
		EndIf
	Else
		This.Value  = ''
		This.Parent.getCor.Value = []
	EndIf
ENDIF

This.Refresh

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mativapagina1
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mativapagina1
Local Array laCtrlgrid1(1)

With ThisForm
	.poDataMgr.RollBack

	If (.plAutoInclusao And .pcEscolha = [INSERIR] And Not .plCancelar)
		.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Click(1)
	Else
		.poDataMgr.ReQuery(1)
		.KeyPreview = .t.
		.Pagina.Lista.Enabled = .t.
		.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Value = 2
		.Pagina.ActivePage = 1
		.pcEscolha = []

		With .Pagina.Lista.Grade
			.Refresh
			.SetFocus
			.Columns(Max(1,.ActiveColumn)).Controls(.Columns(Max(1,.ActiveColumn)).ControlCount).SetFocus
		EndWith
	EndIf 
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mobjenabled
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mobjenabled
LParameters loRef, llChk

Local lnObj

If llChk
	For lnObj=1 To loRef.ControlCount
		If (Inlist(Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass), [TEXTBOX], [OPTIONGROUP], [CHECKBOX], [EDITBOX], [COMBOBOX], [LISTBOX]) And Not Empty(loRef.Controls(lnObj).ClassLibrary))
			If (Inlist(Thisform.pcEscolha, [CONSULTAR], [EXCLUIR]) Or (Thisform.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR] And Not loRef.Controls(lnObj).plProcurar))
				loRef.Controls(lnObj).Enabled = (Not Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass)= [OPTIONGROUP])

				If (Type([loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly])=[L])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly = (Not (ThisForm.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR] And Not loRef.Controls(lnObj).plProcurar))
				EndIf
				
				If Inlist(Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass), [TEXTBOX], [EDITBOX], [COMBOBOX], [LISTBOX])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).DisabledForeColor = loRef.Controls(lnObj).ForeColor
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).DisabledBackColor = loRef.Controls(lnObj).BackColor
				EndIf
				
				If (Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass)= [OPTIONGROUP])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).SetAll([Enabled], .t., [OptionButton])
				EndIf
			Else
				loRef.Controls(lnObj).Enabled = .t.
				If (Type([loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly])=[L])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly = .f.
				EndIf
				
				If (Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass) = [OPTIONGROUP])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).SetAll([Enabled], .t., [OptionButton])
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndFor
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------

EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE KeyPress
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE KeyPress
Lparameters nKeyCode, nShiftAltCtrl

Local loGrp, lnPag

loGrp = This.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op
lnPag = This.Pagina.ActivePage

Do Case
	Case (nKeyCode = 13) And lnPag = 1 And Type([This.ActiveControl.BaseClass]) = [C] And Upper(This.ActiveControl.BaseClass) = [PAGE]
		NoDefault
		
	Case (nKeyCode = 13) And lnPag = 1 And Type([This.Pagina.Lista.ActiveControl.BaseClass]) = [C] And Upper(This.Pagina.Lista.ActiveControl.BaseClass) = [GRID]
		NoDefault
		loGrp.Click(2)

	Case (nKeyCode = -1) And lnPag = 1 And ThisForm.plAcInserir
		NoDefault
		loGrp.Click(1)
		
	Case (nKeyCode = -2) And lnPag = 1 And ThisForm.plAcAlterar
		NoDefault
		loGrp.Click(3)
		
	Case (nKeyCode = -3) And lnPag = 1 And ThisForm.plAcExcluir
		NoDefault
		loGrp.Click(4)
		
	Case (nKeyCode = -4) And lnPag = 1
		NoDefault
		loGrp.Click(5)

	Case (nKeyCode = -7) && Tiago - 01/02/2016 - F8 - Ativa busca por like na classe fwBuscaExt
		Nodefault
		goSistema.BuscaP = .t.
EndCase
* Fim **************************************************************************************

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
LParameters pAce, pTit

Local lnCnt1, lnMax, lnRc1, lnRc2, llLok

With ThisForm
	pAce = Iif(Type([pAce])=[C], pAce, .Name)
	pTit = Iif(Type([pTit])=[C], pTit, .Caption)

	llLok = .LockScreen
	
	.LockScreen = .t.
	.ShowTips   = .t.
	
	.plAcInserir = (.plAcInserir And fChecaAcesso(pAce, [INSERIR]))
	.plAcAlterar = (.plAcAlterar And fChecaAcesso(pAce, [ALTERAR]))
	.plAcExcluir = (.plAcExcluir And fChecaAcesso(pAce, [EXCLUIR]))
	.plAcListar  = .f.
	
	With .Pagina.Lista.Grade
		.Enabled 			= .t.
		.Visible 			= .t.
		.AllowHeaderSizing  = .f.
		.AllowRowSizing 	= .f.
		.DeleteMark 		= .f.
		.ScrollBars 		= 2
		.SetAll([FontName],[Verdana],[Column])
		.SetAll([FontName],[Verdana],[Header])
		.SetAll([FontName],[Verdana],[TextBox])
		.SetAll([FontName],[Verdana],[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([FontSize],8,[Column])
		.SetAll([FontSize],8,[Header])
		.SetAll([FontSize],8,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([FontSize],8,[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Format],[K],[Column])
		.SetAll([Format],[K],[TextBox])
		.SetAll([Format],[K],[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Movable],.f.,[Column])
		.SetAll([ReadOnly],.t.,[Column])
		.SetAll([ReadOnly],.t.,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([ReadOnly],.t.,[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Resizable],.f.,[Column])
		.SetAll([Alignment],3,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([Alignment],3,[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Alignment],3,[fwGrdLocate1])
		.SetAll([Alignment],2,[Header])
		.SetAll([BorderStyle],0,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([BorderStyle],0,[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Margin],0,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([Margin],0,[TextGrade])
		.SetAll([Visible],.t.,[TextBox])
		.SetAll([Visible],.t.,[TextGrade])
	EndWith
	
	With .Pagina.Lista.cntSombra
		pTit = Alltrim(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(pTit,'Cadastro de',''),'Cadastro da',''),'Cadastro do',''))
		.lblSombra.Caption = pTit 
		.lblTitulo.Caption = pTit
	EndWith
	
	With .Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op
		.Enabled = .t.
		.Visible = .t.
		.Inserir.Enabled = ThisForm.plAcInserir
		.Alterar.Enabled = ThisForm.plAcAlterar
		.Excluir.Enabled = ThisForm.plAcExcluir
	EndWith

	.mAtivaPagina1()

	If DoDefault()
		With .Pagina.Lista.Grade
			If Used(.RecordSource)
				lnMax = Int((.Height - .HeaderHeight - Iif(Inlist(.ScrollBars, 1, 3), Sysmetric(8), 0)) / .RowHeight)

				Go Bottom In (.RecordSource)

				lnRc1 = Recno(.RecordSource)

				If Not Eof(.RecordSource)
					Skip -(lnMax - 1) In (.RecordSource)

					If Between(lnRc1, 1, Reccount(.RecordSource))
						lnRc2 = Recno(.RecordSource)

						Go Bottom In (.RecordSource)
						.Refresh()

						Do While .t.
							.ActivateCell(1, 1)
							If (Recno(.RecordSource) = lnRc2)
								Exit
							Else
								.DoScroll(0)
							EndIf 
						EndDo 
						Goto lnRc1 In (.RecordSource)
					EndIf 
				EndIf 
			EndIf 
		EndWith 
	EndIf 
	.LockScreen = llLok
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Load
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Load
=fConfigGeral()

With ThisForm
	.plAcInserir = .t.
	.plAcAlterar = .t.
	.plAcExcluir = .t.
	.plCancelar  = .f.
	.pcEscolha   = []
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Release
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Release
If (Type([This.poDataMgr])=[O])
	This.poDataMgr.Release
EndIf

=DoDefault()
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: frmcadastro.Pagina
* Classe: pageframe (Base: pageframe)
* Registro: 253
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Move
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Move
LPARAMETERS nLeft, nTop, nWidth, nHeight

LOCAL lcWindow, lnLeft, lnTop
lcWindow = IIF(_screen.WindowState = 1, Thisform.Name, '')
lnLeft = This.Left - MCOL(m.lcWindow,3)
lnTop = This.Top - MROW(m.lcWindow,3)

DO WHILE MDOWN()
	This.Move(m.lnLeft + MCOL(m.lcWindow,3), m.lnTop + MROW(m.lcWindow,3))
ENDDO
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Lista.Activate
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Lista.Activate
This.Grade.SetFocus
This.Refresh
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Dados.Activate
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Dados.Activate
Local llLok

llLok = ThisForm.LockScreen

If (Not Type([ThisForm.pcEscolha])=[C] Or Empty(Thisform.pcEscolha))
	ThisForm.LockScreen = .t.
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Value = 2
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op.Click(2)
EndIf

If (Type([ThisForm.pcEscolha]) = [C] And Not Empty(Thisform.pcEscolha))
	ThisForm.Pagina.Lista.Enabled = .f.
	If InList(ThisForm.pcEscolha, [CONSULTAR], [EXCLUIR])
		This.Grupo_Salva.Salva.SetFocus
	EndIf
	
	This.Refresh
EndIf

ThisForm.LockScreen = llLok
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: frmcadastro.Pagina.Lista.Grupo_Op
* Classe: commandgroup (Base: commandgroup)
* Registro: 258
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Click
LParameters lnOpt

Local llRet

If (Type([lnOpt])=[N])
	This.Value = lnOpt
EndIf

llRet = .t.

With ThisForm
	Do Case
		Case (This.Value = 1)
			.pcEscolha = [INSERIR]
			.poDataMgr.NewReg(1, .t.)
			
		Case (This.Value = 2)
			.pcEscolha = [CONSULTAR]
			.poDataMgr.ReQuery(1, .poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria, Evaluate(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor+[.]+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria))
			
		Case (This.Value = 3)
			.pcEscolha = [ALTERAR]
			.poDataMgr.ReQuery(1, .poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria, Evaluate(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor+[.]+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria))
			
		Case (This.Value = 4)
			.pcEscolha = [EXCLUIR]
			.poDataMgr.ReQuery(1, .poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria, Evaluate(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor+[.]+.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcChavePrimaria))

		Case (This.Value = 5)
			.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR]
			If (Used(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor) And Not Eof(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor))
				ThisForm.poDataMgr.NewReg(1)
			EndIf 
	EndCase
	
	.mObjEnabled(.Pagina.Dados, .t.)
	
	If (This.Value <> 0) And (Not Used(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor) Or Not Eof(.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor))
		.KeyPreview = .f.
		.Pagina.Dados.Grupo_Salva.Salva.Enabled = (Not .pcEscolha = [CONSULTAR])
		.Pagina.ActivePage = 2
	Else
		.KeyPreview = .t.
		llRet = .f.
	EndIf
EndWith

Return llRet
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Salva.KeyPress
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Salva.KeyPress
Lparameters nKeyCode, nShiftAltCtrl

If (nKeyCode = 13 And nShiftAltCtrl=0)
	NoDefault
	This.Click()
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Salva.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Salva.Click
With ThisForm
	.plCancelar = .f.

	Do Case
		Case (.pcEscolha = [INSERIR])
			.mSv_Inserir()
			
		Case (.pcEscolha = [CONSULTAR])
			.mSv_Consultar()
			
		Case (.pcEscolha = [ALTERAR])
			.mSv_Alterar()
			
		Case (.pcEscolha = [EXCLUIR])
			If (MessageBox([Deseja Realmente Excluir Esses Dados?], 4+32+256, [ConfirmańŃo de ExclusŃo]) = 6)
				.mSv_Excluir()
			Else
				.plCancelar = .t.
			EndIf
			
		Case (.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR])
			If (Type([ThisForm.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor])=[C] And Used(ThisForm.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor))
				Select (ThisForm.poDataMgr.pfSqlTabela(1).pcNomeCursor)
				Delete
			EndIf
			.mSv_Procurar()
	EndCase
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Cancelar.KeyPress
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Cancelar.KeyPress
Lparameters nKeyCode, nShiftAltCtrl

If (nKeyCode=13 And nShiftAltCtrl=0)
	NoDefault
	This.Click()
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Cancelar.Click
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Cancelar.Click
With ThisForm
	.plCancelar = (Not InList(.pcEscolha, [INSERIR], [ALTERAR]) Or MessageBox([Confirma o Cancelamento Dos Dados Informados?], 4+32+256, [ConfirmańŃo de Cancelamento])=6)
EndWith
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC


================================================================================
* OBJETO: fwbuscasel
* Classe: form (Base: form)
* Registro: 263
================================================================================

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE addcoluna
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE addcoluna
Lparameters pColCampo,pColMascara,pColTitulo,pColIngrid,pColIndice, pColfilter,pColprefix, pColPadl

If Type( 'pColMascara' ) # 'C'
	pColMascara = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColTitulo' ) # 'C'
	pColTitulo = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColIndice' ) # 'C'
	pColIndice = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColfilter' ) # 'C'
	pColfilter = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColprefix' ) # 'C'
	pColprefix = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColpadl' ) # 'N' Or pColpadl < 0
	pColpadl = 0
Endif
lTamanho = IIF(LEN(pColMascara)>2 OR not INLIST(TYPE(pColCampo),"C","D"),;
	LEN(pColMascara), IIF(TYPE(pColCampo)=="C",LEN(EVALUATE(pColCampo)),10))
TamGrade=THISFORM.GridProc.width

With THISFORM.GridProc
	NoCol=THISFORM.GridProc.ColumnCount+1
	IF NoCol=0
		NoCol=1
	Endif
	.AddColumn(NoCol)
	NoColuna=alltrim(str(THISFORM.GridProc.ColumnCount,20))
EndWith

This.cKeyFiltro = pColfilter
This.cPrefixo = pColprefix

With THISFORM.GridProc
	.Column&NoColuna..ControlSource = Iif(At(Alltrim(This.gArquivo),AllTrim(pColCampo))>0,;
	                                      AllTrim(pColCampo),;
	                                      (Alltrim(This.gArquivo)+'.'+AllTrim(pColCampo)))
	.Column&NoColuna..width = INT((lTamanho*7)+10)
	.Column&NoColuna..Movable=.f.
	.Column&NoColuna..Resizable=.f.
	.Column&NoColuna..Format='K'
	.Column&NoColuna..SelectOnEntry=.f.
	.Column&NoColuna..FontName='Courier New'
	.Column&NoColuna..Header1.Caption= Alltrim(pColTitulo) 
	.Column&NoColuna..Header1.FontName='Arial'
	.Column&NoColuna..Header1.Alignment=2
	.Column&NoColuna..AddObject("Ingrid1","Ingrid")
	.Column&NoColuna..CurrentControl='Ingrid1'
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.ListaProc=.t.
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.lingridactive=pcolIngrid
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cseektag=pColIndice
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cordertag=pColIndice	
	If !Empty( This.cKeyFiltro )
		.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cKeyFilter='ThisForm.cKeyFiltro'
	Else
		.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cKeyFilter=''
	Endif
	If !Empty( This.cPrefixo )
		.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cprefixseek=iif(at(".",ThisForm.cPrefixo)>0,ThisForm.cPrefixo,'ThisForm.cPrefixo') 
	Else
		.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.cprefixseek=''
	Endif
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.Visible=.T.
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.Lsearchpreview=.F.
	.Column&NoColuna..Ingrid1.nPadl=pColPadl
	.Column&NoColuna..RemoveObject("Text1")
	.Column&NoColuna..ReadOnly=.T.
	.width = THISFORM.GridProc.Column&NoColuna..width+TamGrade+5
	this.width = THISFORM.GridProc.width+5
EndWith
THISFORM.GridProc.Refresh




ENDPROC

PROCEDURE Init
LPARAMETERS pArquivo,pIndice,pBusca,pTitulo

this.gAlias = SELECT()
this.gOrder = ORDER()
IF TYPE("pArquivo")<>"C" OR not USED(pArquivo)
	RETURN(.F.)
ENDIF
This.gArquivo=pArquivo
SELECT (pArquivo)
this.gOrdArq = ORDER()
IF TYPE("pIndice")=="C"
	SET ORDER TO (pIndice)
ENDIF
IF !EMPTY(pBusca)
	SET NEAR ON
	SEEK IIF(TYPE("pBusca")=="C",ALLTRIM(pBusca),pBusca)
	SET NEAR OFF
ENDIF
IF TYPE("pTitulo")=="C"
	this.caption = Alltrim( pTitulo )
EndIf

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = ThisForm.Caption
ThisForm.cntSombra.lblTitulo.Caption = ThisForm.Caption

this.controlbox = .F.
this.windowtype = 1
SELECT (pArquivo)
This.Height=330
WITH this.GridProc
	.height = 200
	.recordsource = pArquivo
	.columncount=0
	.scrollbars = 2
	.readonly=.T.
ENDWITH
this.autocenter = .T.

ENDPROC

	SELECT (thisform.GridProc.recordsource)

		SET ORDER TO (thisform.gOrdArq)
	Endif
Endif
If thisform.gAlias > 0
	SELECT (thisform.gAlias)
	If not empty(Thisform.gOrder)
		Set Order to (Thisform.gOrder)
	Endif
Endif
ON KEY LABEL ESCAPE

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE maddcoluna
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE maddcoluna
Lparameters pColCampo,pColMascara,pColTitulo,llIngrid
Local lcMcrCol1,lcCtrlSource,lcMcrTag1,lnNreg1

If Type( 'pColMascara' ) # 'C'
	pColMascara = ''
Endif
If Type( 'pColTitulo' ) # 'C'
	pColTitulo = ''
Endif
lTamanho = IIF(LEN(pColMascara)>2 OR not INLIST(TYPE(pColCampo),"C","D"),;
	LEN(pColMascara), IIF(TYPE(pColCampo)=="C",LEN(EVALUATE(pColCampo)),10))

m.lnNreg1 = Recno(This.gcArquivo)
With ThisForm.GridProc
	NoCol=ThisForm.GridProc.ColumnCount+1
	IF NoCol=0
		NoCol=1
	Endif
	.AddColumn(NoCol)
	lcMcrCol1=alltrim(str(ThisForm.GridProc.ColumnCount,20))
EndWith
If InList(Type(Alltrim(This.gcArquivo)+'.'+AllTrim(pColCampo)),'N','C','D','T') And llIngrid
	m.lcMcrTag1 = AllTrim(pColCampo)
	Select (This.gcArquivo)
	Index On &lcMcrTag1. Tag &lcMcrTag1.
	Set Order To ('') In (This.gcArquivo)
EndIf 
With This
	With .GridProc
		m.lcCtrlSource = Iif(At(Lower(Alltrim(This.gcArquivo)),Lower(AllTrim(pColCampo)))>0,;
		                     AllTrim(pColCampo),;
		                     (Alltrim(This.gcArquivo)+'.'+AllTrim(pColCampo)))
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..ControlSource = m.lcCtrlSource
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Width = INT((lTamanho*7)+10)
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Movable = .f.
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Resizable = .f.
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Format = 'K'
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..InputMask=Iif((.Not.Type(m.lcCtrlSource)=='N'.Or.Lower(Left(pColMascara,1))=='9'),pColMascara,'')
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..SelectOnEntry = .f.
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..FontName = 'Courier New'
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..FontSize = 9
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Alignment = 3
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.Caption= Alltrim(pColTitulo) && Upper(Substr(pColTitulo,1,1))+Substr(pColTitulo,2)
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.FontName = 'Arial'
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.FontSize = 8
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.Alignment = 2
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..AddObject("ingrid1","fwGrdLocate1",.t.)
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..CurrentControl = 'ingrid1'
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..RemoveObject("Text1")
		.Column&lcMcrCol1..ReadOnly = .T.
		With .Column&lcMcrCol1..ingrid1
			.Visible = .t.
			.Format = 'K'
			.InputMask = m.pColMascara
			.FontName = 'Courier New'
			.FontSize = 9
			.Alignment = 3
			.BorderStyle = 0
			.Margin = 0
			.Height = 25
			.Width = 100
			.ckeyfilter = ''
			.clocateexpression = ''
			.cordertag = ''
			.cprefixseek = ''
			.csearchstring = ''
			.cseektag = ''
			.lingridactive = m.llIngrid

			If .lingridactive
				.cordertag = m.lcMcrTag1
				.cseektag  = m.lcMcrTag1
			EndIf 
			.nwaittime = (_DblClick)
		EndWith
	EndWith
EndWith
If Between(m.lnNreg1,1,Reccount(This.gcArquivo))
	Goto m.lnNreg1 In (This.gcArquivo)
EndIf 

ENDPROC

		EndFor
		.SetAll('DynamicBackColor','Iif(RecNo(This.RecordSource)==This.Parent.pnRecno1,RGB(0,255,255),RGB(255,255,255))','Column')
		.Refresh
	EndWith

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
LPARAMETERS pArquivo,pCampo,pBusca,pTitulo,pTudo,pOrdem,pProds

Local lBusca

this.gAlias = SELECT()
IF TYPE("pArquivo")<>"C" OR not USED(pArquivo)
	RETURN(.F.)
ENDIF
pOrdem = IIF((Type("pOrdem")<>"C" or Type("pOrdem")<>"N") and !empty(pOrdem),pOrdem,pCampo)
This.gArquivo=alltrim(pArquivo)
This.gCampo=pCampo
SELECT (pArquivo)
This.gOrdArq = ORDER()
lBusca = pBusca
If Used('crTmpArquivo')
	USE In ('crTmpArquivo')
EndIf 
IF TYPE("pBusca")=="C" and !pTudo
	pBusca=ALLTRIM(pBusca)
	pBusca=StrTran(pBusca,"'","")
	Select * from (pArquivo) Where &pCampo. Like "%&pBusca.%" into cursor crTmpArquivo ;
					order by &pOrdem.
Endif
IF TYPE("pBusca")=="N" and !pTudo
	pBusca=ALLTRIM(STR(pBusca,20))
	Select * from (pArquivo) Where Alltrim(Str(&pCampo.,20)) Like "&pBusca.%" ;
			into cursor crTmpArquivo order by &pOrdem. 
Endif
IF TYPE("pTudo")=="L" and pTudo
	Select * from (pArquivo) into cursor crTmpArquivo order by &pOrdem.
Endif
If Used('cArquivo')
	USE In ('cArquivo')
EndIf 
USE Dbf('crTmpArquivo') Alias ('cArquivo') Again In 0
This.gcArquivo='cArquivo'
IF TYPE("pTitulo")=="C"
	this.caption = Alltrim( pTitulo )&& Upper(Substr(pTitulo,1,1))+Substr(pTitulo,2)
EndIf

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = ThisForm.Caption
ThisForm.cntSombra.lblTitulo.Caption = ThisForm.Caption

this.controlbox = .F.
this.windowtype = 1
SELECT cArquivo
IF !EMPTY(pBusca)
	Locate
	Locate for evaluate(pCampo) >= IIF(TYPE("lBusca")=="C",ALLTRIM(lBusca),lBusca)
EndIf
This.Height=335
WITH this.GridProc
	.height = 240
	.recordsource = 'cArquivo'
	.columncount=0
	.scrollbars = 2
	.readonly=.T.
EndWith
This.pnRecno1 = 0
this.autocenter = .T.

This.cntProds.Visible = .f.
If (Type([pProds]) = [C]) And Not Empty(pProds)
	This.poDataMgr = CreateObject([fSqlConector], This.Name)
	If (This.poDataMgr.pnIdconn > 0)
		This.CampoChave = pProds
		This.cntProds.Visible = .t.
		This.Height = This.Height + This.cntProds.Height + 5
		This.cntProds.Top  = This.gridProc.Top + This.gridProc.Height + 2
		This.cntProds.Left = This.gridProc.Left
	EndIf
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************


ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Hide
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Hide
If (Type([This.poDataMgr]) = [O])
	This.poDataMgr.Release
EndIf

If not empty(ThisForm.GridProc.recordsource)
	SELECT (ThisForm.GridProc.recordsource)
Endif
If not empty(ThisForm.gArquivo)
	SELECT (ThisForm.gArquivo)
Endif

lcmacro1 = (ThisForm.gArquivo+'.'+alltrim(ThisForm.gCampo))
lcmacro2 = Alltrim(ThisForm.gcArquivo)+'.'+alltrim(ThisForm.gCampo)
Locate for &lcmacro1. = &lcmacro2.

If ThisForm.gAlias > 0
	SELECT (ThisForm.gAlias)
EndIf 

ON KEY LABEL ESCAPE

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE AfterRowColChange
LPARAMETERS nColIndex
This.Refresh

If This.Parent.cntProds.Visible And Not Empty(This.Parent.CampoChave)
	This.Parent.cntProds.getLinha.Value     = []
	This.Parent.cntProds.getColecao.Value   = []
	This.Parent.cntProds.getClFiscals.Value = []

	lcCpo = Alltrim(This.RecordSource) + [.] + Alltrim(This.Parent.CampoChave)
	lcBus = &lcCpo.

	lcQuery = [Select a.Linhas, b.Descs as DLins, a.Colecoes, c.Descs as DCols, ] + ;
					 [a.ClFiscals, d.Descricaos as DCFis, a.pvens ] + ;
			    [From SigcdPro a ] + ;
		   [Left Join SigCdLin b On a.Linhas = b.Linhas ] + ;
		   [Left Join SigCdCol c On a.Colecoes = c.Colecoes ] + ;
		   [Left Join SigCdClf d On a.ClFiscals = d.Codigos ] + ;
			   [Where a.CPros = '] + lcBus + [']

	If (This.Parent.poDataMgr.SqlExecute(lcQuery, [LocalPro3]) < 1)
		=MessageBox([Favor Reinicializar o Processo!!!], 16, [Falha na ConexŃo (LocalPro3)])
		Return 0
	ENDIF

	*** Mena - 03/02/2014 - mostra vr substituicao e IPI
	lnValSubs = 0
	lnValIPI  = 0
	lcCpo = Alltrim(This.RecordSource) + [.] + [pvens]
	IF TYPE(lcCpo) <> 'U'	&& verifica se existe o campo
		lcPv  = &lcCpo.
		lnValSubs = fCalcularST(lcBus, TprMvCab.contaDs, lcPv, TprMvCab.fpubls, TprMvCab.emps)
		lnValIPI  = fCalcularIPI(lcBus, TprMvCab.contaDs, lcPv, TprMvCab.fpubls, TprMvCab.emps)
	ENDIF
		
	This.Parent.cntProds.getLinha.Value     = Alltrim(LocalPro3.Linhas)    + [-] + Nvl(LocalPro3.DLins, [])
	This.Parent.cntProds.getColecao.Value   = Alltrim(LocalPro3.Colecoes)  + [-] + Nvl(LocalPro3.DCols, [])
	This.Parent.cntProds.getClFiscals.Value = Alltrim(LocalPro3.ClFiscals) + [-] + Nvl(LocalPro3.DCFis, [])
	This.Parent.cntProds.getSubst.Value =     Alltrim(transform(lnValSubs, '999999.99'))
	This.Parent.cntProds.getIPI.Value =     Alltrim(transform(lnValIPI, '999999.99'))
	This.Parent.cntProds.getLinha.Refresh
	This.Parent.cntProds.getColecao.Refresh
	This.Parent.cntProds.getClFiscals.Refresh
	This.Parent.cntProds.getSubst.Refresh
	This.Parent.cntProds.getIPI.Refresh
	Use In LocalPro3
	lcCpo = Alltrim(This.Parent.gArquivo)
	Select &lcCpo.
ENDIF

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE DblClick
thisform.hide
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE loadregfuncs
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE loadregfuncs
* Loads funtions needed for Registry
LOCAL nHKey,cSubKey,nResult
LOCAL hKey,iValue,lpszValue,lpcchValue,lpdwType,lpbData,lpcbData
LOCAL lpcStr,lpszVal,nLen,lpdwReserved
LOCAL lpszValueName,dwReserved,fdwType
LOCAL iSubKey,lpszName,cchName

IF THIS.lLoadedDLLs
	RETURN ERROR_SUCCESS
ENDIF

DECLARE Integer RegOpenKey IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey, String @cSubKey, Integer @nResult

IF THIS.lhaderror && error loading library
	RETURN -1
ENDIF

DECLARE Integer RegCreateKey IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey, String @cSubKey, Integer @nResult

DECLARE Integer RegDeleteKey IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey, String @cSubKey

DECLARE Integer RegDeleteValue IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey, String cSubKey

DECLARE Integer RegCloseKey IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey

DECLARE Integer RegSetValueEx IN Win32API ;
	Integer hKey, String lpszValueName, Integer dwReserved,;
	Integer fdwType, String lpbData, Integer cbData

DECLARE Integer RegQueryValueEx IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey, String lpszValueName, Integer dwReserved,;
	Integer @lpdwType, String @lpbData, Integer @lpcbData

DECLARE Integer RegEnumKey IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey,Integer iSubKey, String @lpszName, Integer @cchName

DECLARE Integer RegEnumKeyEx IN Win32API ;
	Integer nHKey,Integer iSubKey, String @lpszName, Integer @cchName,;
	Integer dwReserved,String @lpszName, Integer @cchName,String @cchName

DECLARE Integer RegEnumValue IN Win32API ;
	Integer hKey, Integer iValue, String @lpszValue, ;
	Integer @lpcchValue, Integer lpdwReserved, Integer @lpdwType, ;
	String @lpbData, Integer @lpcbData
    		
THIS.lLoadedDLLs = .T.

* Need error check here
RETURN ERROR_SUCCESS

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE openkey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE openkey
* Opens a registry key
LPARAMETER cLookUpKey,nRegKey,lCreateKey

LOCAL nSubKey,nErrCode,nPCount,lSaveCreateKey
nSubKey = 0
nPCount = PARAMETERS()

IF TYPE("m.nRegKey") # "N" OR EMPTY(m.nRegKey)
	m.nRegKey = HKEY_CLASSES_ROOT
ENDIF

* Load API functions
nErrCode = THIS.LoadRegFuncs()
IF m.nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrCode
ENDIF

lSaveCreateKey = THIS.lCreateKey
IF m.nPCount>2 AND TYPE("m.lCreateKey") = "L"
	THIS.lCreateKey = m.lCreateKey
ENDIF
Try 
	IF THIS.lCreateKey
		* Try to open or create registry key
		nErrCode = RegCreateKey(m.nRegKey,m.cLookUpKey,@nSubKey)
	ELSE
		* Try to open registry key
		nErrCode = RegOpenKey(m.nRegKey,m.cLookUpKey,@nSubKey)
	ENDIF
Catch
	nErrCode = 0
EndTry 
THIS.lCreateKey = m.lSaveCreateKey

IF nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrCode
ENDIF

THIS.nCurrentKey = m.nSubKey
RETURN ERROR_SUCCESS

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE closekey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE closekey
* Closes a registry key
=RegCloseKey(THIS.nCurrentKey)
THIS.nCurrentKey =0 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE setregkey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE setregkey
* This routine sets a registry key setting
* ex. THIS.SetRegKey("ResWidth","640",;
*		"Software\Microsoft\VisualFoxPro\6.0\Options",;
*		HKEY_CURRENT_USER)
LPARAMETER cOptName,cOptVal,cKeyPath,nUserKey,lCreateKey
LOCAL iPos,cOptKey,cOption,nErrNum
iPos = 0
cOption = ""
nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

* Open registry key
m.nErrNum = THIS.OpenKey(m.cKeyPath,m.nUserKey,m.lCreateKey)
IF m.nErrNum # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrNum
ENDIF

* Set Key value
nErrNum = THIS.SetKeyValue(m.cOptName,m.cOptVal)

* Close registry key 
THIS.CloseKey()		&&close key
RETURN m.nErrNum

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE getregkey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE getregkey
* This routine gets a registry key setting
* ex. THIS.GetRegKey("ResWidth",@cValue,;
*		"Software\Microsoft\VisualFoxPro\4.0\Options",;
*		HKEY_CURRENT_USER)
LPARAMETER cOptName,cOptVal,cKeyPath,nUserKey
LOCAL iPos,cOptKey,cOption,nErrNum
iPos = 0
cOption = ""
nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

* Open registry key
m.nErrNum = THIS.OpenKey(m.cKeyPath,m.nUserKey)
IF m.nErrNum # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrNum
ENDIF

* Get the key value
nErrNum = THIS.GetKeyValue(cOptName,@cOptVal)

* Close registry key 
THIS.CloseKey()		&&close key
RETURN m.nErrNum

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE getkeyvalue
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE getkeyvalue
* Obtains a value from a registry key
* Note: this routine only handles Data strings (REG_SZ)
LPARAMETER cValueName,cKeyValue

LOCAL lpdwReserved,lpdwType,lpbData,lpcbData,nErrCode
STORE 0 TO lpdwReserved,lpdwType
STORE SPACE(256) TO lpbData
STORE LEN(m.lpbData) TO m.lpcbData

DO CASE
CASE TYPE("THIS.nCurrentKey")#'N' OR THIS.nCurrentKey = 0
	RETURN ERROR_BADKEY
CASE TYPE("m.cValueName") #"C"
	RETURN ERROR_BADPARM
ENDCASE

m.nErrCode=RegQueryValueEx(THIS.nCurrentKey,m.cValueName,;
		m.lpdwReserved,@lpdwType,@lpbData,@lpcbData)

* Check for error 
IF m.nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrCode
ENDIF

* Make sure we have a data string data type
IF m.lpdwType # REG_SZ AND m.lpdwType # REG_EXPAND_SZ 
	RETURN ERROR_NONSTR_DATA		
ENDIF

m.cKeyValue = LEFT(m.lpbData,m.lpcbData-1)
RETURN ERROR_SUCCESS

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE setkeyvalue
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE setkeyvalue
* This routine sets a key value
* Note: this routine only handles data strings (REG_SZ)
LPARAMETER cValueName,cValue
LOCAL nValueSize,nErrCode 

DO CASE
CASE TYPE("THIS.nCurrentKey")#'N' OR THIS.nCurrentKey = 0
	RETURN ERROR_BADKEY
CASE TYPE("m.cValueName") #"C" OR TYPE("m.cValue")#"C"
	RETURN ERROR_BADPARM
CASE EMPTY(m.cValueName) OR EMPTY(m.cValue)
	* RETURN ERROR_BADPARM
ENDCASE

* Make sure we null terminate this guy
cValue = m.cValue+CHR(0)
nValueSize = LEN(m.cValue)

* Set the key value here
m.nErrCode = RegSetValueEx(THIS.nCurrentKey,m.cValueName,0,;
	REG_SZ,m.cValue,m.nValueSize)

* Check for error
IF m.nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrCode
ENDIF

RETURN ERROR_SUCCESS

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE deletekey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE deletekey
* This routine deletes a Registry Key
LPARAMETER nUserKey,cKeyPath
LOCAL nErrNum
nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

* Delete key
m.nErrNum = RegDeleteKey(m.nUserKey,m.cKeyPath)
RETURN m.nErrNum

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE enumoptions
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE enumoptions
* Enumerates through all entries for a key and populates array
LPARAMETER aRegOpts,cOptPath,nUserKey,lEnumKeys
LOCAL iPos,cOptKey,cOption,nErrNum
iPos = 0
cOption = ""
nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

IF PARAMETERS()<4 OR TYPE("m.lEnumKeys") # "L"
	lEnumKeys = .F.
ENDIF

* Open key
m.nErrNum = THIS.OpenKey(m.cOptPath,m.nUserKey)
IF m.nErrNum # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrNum
ENDIF

* Enumerate through keys
IF m.lEnumKeys
	* Enumerate and get key names
	nErrNum = THIS.EnumKeys(@aRegOpts)
ELSE
	* Enumerate and get all key values
	nErrNum = THIS.EnumKeyValues(@aRegOpts)
ENDIF

* Close key
THIS.CloseKey()		&&close key
RETURN m.nErrNum

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE iskey
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE iskey
* Checks to see if a key exists
LPARAMETER cKeyName,nRegKey
LOCAL nErrNum 
* Open extension key

nErrCode = THIS.LoadRegFuncs()		
nErrNum = THIS.OpenKey(m.cKeyName,m.nRegKey)

If Type([nErrNum])<>[N]
	nErrNum = 0
EndIf 

IF m.nErrNum  = ERROR_SUCCESS
	* Close extension key
	THIS.CloseKey()
ENDIF

RETURN m.nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE enumkeys
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE enumkeys
PARAMETER aKeyNames
LOCAL nKeyEntry,cNewKey,cNewSize,cbuf,nbuflen,cRetTime
nKeyEntry = 0
DIMENSION aKeyNames[1]
DO WHILE .T.
	nKeySize = 0
	cNewKey = SPACE(100)
	nKeySize = LEN(m.cNewKey)
	cbuf=space(100)
	nbuflen=len(m.cbuf)
	cRetTime=space(100)

	m.nErrCode = RegEnumKeyEx(THIS.nCurrentKey,m.nKeyEntry,@cNewKey,@nKeySize,0,@cbuf,@nbuflen,@cRetTime)
	
	DO CASE
	CASE m.nErrCode = ERROR_EOF
		EXIT
	CASE m.nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
		EXIT
	ENDCASE

	cNewKey = ALLTRIM(m.cNewKey)
	cNewKey = LEFT(m.cNewKey,LEN(m.cNewKey)-1)
	IF !EMPTY(aKeyNames[1])
		DIMENSION aKeyNames[ALEN(aKeyNames)+1]
	ENDIF
	aKeyNames[ALEN(aKeyNames)] = m.cNewKey 
	nKeyEntry = m.nKeyEntry + 1
ENDDO

IF m.nErrCode = ERROR_EOF AND m.nKeyEntry # 0
	m.nErrCode = ERROR_SUCCESS
ENDIF
RETURN m.nErrCode

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE enumkeyvalues
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE enumkeyvalues
* Enumerates through values of a registry key
LPARAMETER aKeyValues

LOCAL lpszValue,lpcchValue,lpdwReserved
LOCAL lpdwType,lpbData,lpcbData
LOCAL nErrCode,nKeyEntry,lArrayPassed

STORE 0 TO nKeyEntry

IF TYPE("THIS.nCurrentKey")#'N' OR THIS.nCurrentKey = 0
	RETURN ERROR_BADKEY
ENDIF

* Sorry, Win32s does not support this one!
IF THIS.nCurrentOS = OS_W32S
	RETURN ERROR_BADPLAT
ENDIF

DO WHILE .T.

	STORE 0 TO lpdwReserved,lpdwType,nErrCode
	STORE SPACE(256) TO lpbData, lpszValue
	STORE LEN(lpbData) TO m.lpcchValue
	STORE LEN(lpszValue) TO m.lpcbData

	nErrCode=RegEnumValue(THIS.nCurrentKey,m.nKeyEntry,@lpszValue,;
		@lpcchValue,m.lpdwReserved,@lpdwType,@lpbData,@lpcbData)
	
	DO CASE
	CASE m.nErrCode = ERROR_EOF
		EXIT
	CASE m.nErrCode # ERROR_SUCCESS
		EXIT
	ENDCASE

	nKeyEntry = m.nKeyEntry + 1

	* Set array values
	DIMENSION aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,2]
	aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,1] = LEFT(m.lpszValue,m.lpcchValue)
	DO CASE
	CASE lpdwType = REG_SZ
		aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,2] = LEFT(m.lpbData,m.lpcbData-1)
	CASE lpdwType = REG_BINARY
		* Don't support binary
		aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,2] = REG_BINARY_LOC
	CASE lpdwType = REG_DWORD
		* You will need to use ASC() to check values here.
		aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,2] = LEFT(m.lpbData,m.lpcbData-1)
	OTHERWISE
		aKeyValues[m.nKeyEntry,2] = REG_UNKNOWN_LOC
	ENDCASE
ENDDO
 
IF m.nErrCode = ERROR_EOF AND m.nKeyEntry # 0
	m.nErrCode = ERROR_SUCCESS
ENDIF
RETURN m.nErrCode

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE deletekeyvalue
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE deletekeyvalue
LPARAMETER cOptName,cKeyPath,nUserKey
LOCAL cOption,nErrNum
cOption = cOptName
nErrNum = ERROR_SUCCESS

* Open key
m.nErrNum = THIS.OpenKey(m.cKeyPath,m.nUserKey)
IF m.nErrNum # ERROR_SUCCESS
	RETURN m.nErrNum
ENDIF

* Delete the key value
m.nErrNum = RegDeleteValue(THIS.nCurrentKey,m.cOption)

* Close key
THIS.CloseKey()		&& close key
RETURN m.nErrNum

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init
#Include Registry.h

THIS.nUserKey = HKEY_CURRENT_USER
THIS.cVFPOptPath = VFP_OPTIONS_KEY1 + _VFP.VERSION + VFP_OPTIONS_KEY2
DO CASE
	CASE _DOS OR _UNIX OR _MAC
		RETURN .F.
	CASE ATC("Windows 3",OS(1)) # 0
		THIS.nCurrentOS = OS_W32S
	CASE ATC("Windows NT",OS(1)) # 0
		THIS.nCurrentOS = OS_NT
		THIS.cRegDLLFile = DLL_ADVAPI_NT
		THIS.cINIDLLFile = DLL_KERNEL_NT	
		THIS.cODBCDLLFile = DLL_ODBC_NT
	OTHERWISE
		* Windows 95
		THIS.nCurrentOS = OS_WIN95
		THIS.cRegDLLFile = DLL_ADVAPI_WIN95
		THIS.cINIDLLFile = DLL_KERNEL_WIN95
		THIS.cODBCDLLFile = DLL_ODBC_WIN95
ENDCASE

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Error
LPARAMETERS nError, cMethod, nLine
THIS.lhaderror = .T.
=MESSAGEBOX(MESSAGE())

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE documentoexcel
Local lcExl, lcErr, llErr

llErr = .f.
lcErr = On([Error])
On Error llErr = .t.

lcExl = thisform.pcarqemail

If fVerificaPasta(lcExl, 2)
	If (Lower(Alltrim(JustExt(lcExl))) = [xls])
		Copy To (lcExl) Type Xl5
	Else 
		Copy To (lcExl) Delimited With '' With Character ';'
	EndIf 
Else
	llErr = .t.
EndIf
On Error &lcErr.
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE memail
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE memail
***************************************************
****** Envia email automatico             *********
***************************************************
LParameters tcFrom As String, tcTo As String, tcCC As String, tcAssunto As String, tcCorpo As String, tcAnexo As String, ;
			tcSmtpServer As String, tnSmtpServerPort As Integer, tcSendUserName As String, tcSendPassWord As String


Local loEmail As CDO.Message, llOk As Boolean, llEnvioOK As Boolean 

If Type( 'CreateObject("CDO.Message")' ) # "O"
	MessageBox( "Problemas para instanciar o obj CDO.Message", 48, "AtenńŃo" )
	Return( .F. )
EndIf

loEmail = CreateObject("CDO.Message")

With loEmail.Configuration.Fields
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/sendusing") 			  = 2
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/smtpserver") 			  = Lower( tcSmtpServer )
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/smtpconnectiontimeout") = 10
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/smtpserverport") 		  = Iif( tnSmtpServerPort = 0, 25, tnSmtpServerPort )
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/smtpauthenticate") 	  = 1
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/sendusername") 		  = Lower( tcSendUserName )
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/sendpassword") 		  = tcSendPassWord 
	.Item("http://schemas.microsoft.com/cdo/configuration/smtpusessl")	 		  = Iif( tnSmtpServerPort = 465, 1, 0 ) && mena-05/03/2014 incluido para funcionar com gmail - gmail a porta ķ 465
	.Update()
EndWith

llEnvioOK = .T.

With loEmail
	.To 	  = Lower( tcTo )
	.Cc 	  = Lower( Nvl( tcCC, "" ) )
	.From 	  = Lower( tcFrom )
	.Subject  = AllTrim( tcAssunto )
	.TextBody = AllTrim( tcCorpo )

	****adiciona anexos ****
	If !IsNull( tcAnexo ) And !Empty( tcAnexo )
		If File( tcAnexo )
			.AddAttachment(tcAnexo)
		Else
			llEnvioOK = .F.
			MessageBox( "NŃo foi encontrado o arquivo:" +Chr(13)+ tcAnexo + " para ser anexado.", 48, "AtenńŃo" )
		EndIf
	EndIf

	Try
		If llEnvioOK = .T.
			.Send()
			llOk = .T.
		EndIf
	Catch
		Wait Window "Dados do e-mail invßlidos." TimeOut 5
		llOk = .F.
	EndTry

EndWith

Release oEmail

Return llOk

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE geracatalogo
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE geracatalogo
*** Tiago - 23/11/2015
*** Ferramenta para gerar catßlogo dos produtos relacionados no cursor informado na propriedade pcatalogo

If Empty(Thisform.pcatalogo)
	Return .f.
Endif
If MessageBox('Deseja gerar catßlogo',4+32+256,'Catßlogo') = 7
	Return .f.
Endif

lcTabela = Thisform.pcatalogo
llOk = .F.
If Used(lcTabela) And Reccount(lcTabela) > 0
	If MessageBox('Existem Dados Processados. Deseja Processar novamente?',4+32+256,'') = 6
		llOk = ThisForm.Processamento()
	EndIf
Else
	llOk = ThisForm.Processamento()
EndIf

If Used(lcTabela) And Reccount(lcTabela) > 0 And Type('&lcTabela..Cpros') = 'C'
	Select Distinct Cpros from &lcTabela. Where !Empty(Cpros) into Cursor crCatalogo ReadWrite
	If Reccount([crCatalogo]) > 0
		Do Form SigOpPec With Thisform, .t.
	Endif
Endif
ENDPROC

	thisform.GeraCatalogo()
Endif

If nKeyCode = -7 && Tiago - 01/02/2016 - F8 - Ativa busca por like na classe fwBuscaExt
	goSistema.BuscaP = .t.
Endif

ENDPROC

pTit = Alltrim(Strtran(Strtran(Strtran(pTit,'Relatorio de',''),'Relatorio da',''),'Relatorio do',''))

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = pTit

	With .Imprime

	EndWith
EndWith

PROCEDURE Click
Local lcFil, llRet, lnJpg, lcSep, lcPnt

lcSep = Set([Separator])
lcPnt = Set([Point])

If InList(goSistema.QtdDecimais, 0, 2)
	Set Separator To [,]
	Set Point To [.]
Else
	Set Separator To [.]
	Set Point To [,]
EndIf 

If (This.Value = 4) && Encerrar
	Set Separator To (lcSep)
	Set Point To (lcPnt)

	ThisForm.Release

	Return .t.
Else
	goSistema.ControlaImp = .f.

	If (((This.Value = 2) And Not ThisForm.lAcImprimir) Or ;
		((This.Value = 3) And Not ThisForm.lAcExcel))

		Set Separator To (lcSep)
		Set Point To (lcPnt)

		Return .T.
	EndIf
EndIf

llRet = ThisForm.Processamento()

llRet = Iif(Type([llRet]) = [L], llRet, .t.)

If llRet
	If (Used() And Not Eof())
		Do Case
			Case (This.Value = 1) && VĒdeo
				=fInibirBtn(ThisForm.btnReport.Imprime.Enabled)
				Set Sysmenu Off
				Define Window Visualizar From 0, 0 To 37, 80 Title [ ] + Alltrim(Prompt()) + [ ]
				ThisForm.Visualizacao()
				Release Window Visualizar
				Set Sysmenu On

			Case (This.Value = 2) And ThisForm.lAcImprimir && Impressora
				ThisForm.Impressao()

			Case (This.Value = 3) And ThisForm.lAcExcel && Excel
				lcTabela = Alias()
				Thisform.pcArqEmail = []
				Do form SigPrPdf With thisform
				Select (lcTabela)
				
				If !Empty(Thisform.pcArqEmail)
					If File(Thisform.pcArqEmail) And Messagebox([Jß existe o arquivo ] + Thisform.pcArqEmail + [. Deseja continuar?],4+32+256,[GerańŃo Arquivo]) = 7
						Return .f.
					Endif
					
					If Inlist(Lower(Alltrim(JustExt(Thisform.pcArqEmail))),[xls],[txt])
						ThisForm.DocumentoExcel()
						lPrintPDFCreator = .t.
					Else
						lPrintPDFCreator = fGerPDFCreator(ThisForm)				
*!*							Declare INTEGER Sleep IN WIN32API INTEGER nMilliseconds			
*!*							lPrintPDFCreator = .t.
*!*							lcDefaultPrinter = SET( "PRINTER", 2 )

*!*							If ThisForm.Registry1.IsKey([PDFCreator.clsPDFCreator])
*!*								Thisform.oPdf = CREATEOBJECT("PDFCreator.clsPDFCreator", "PDFCreator_")

*!*								If Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Number") <> 0
*!*									lPrintPDFCreator = .F.
*!*									MessageBox( "Problemas para gerar o obj PDFCretor" +Chr(13) +;
*!*												"ErrorNr: " + Str( Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Number"), 3 ) +Chr(13) +;
*!*												"Descr: " 	+ Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Description"), 48, "AtenńŃo" )
*!*								Else
*!*									Wait Window Chr(13) + [Aguarde... Gerando o Arquivo PDF] + Chr(13) Nowait NoClear				
*!*									
*!*									With Thisform.oPdf
*!*										.cClearCache()
*!*										.cErrorClear()

*!*										llPDFStart = .cStart("/NoProcessingAtStartup")
*!*										If llPDFStart = .F.
*!*											lPrintPDFCreator = .F.

*!*											MessageBox( "Problemas no START do PDFCreator" +Chr(13) +;
*!*														"ErrorNr: " + Str( Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Number"), 3 ) +Chr(13) +;
*!*														"Descr: " 	+ Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Description"), 48, "AtenńŃo" )
*!*										Else
*!*								**			.cVisible = .F.

*!*											.cOption("UpdateInterval")		 = 0

*!*											.cOption("UseAutosaveDirectory") = 1

*!*											.cOption("StandardTitle") 		 = ""

*!*											.cOption("AutosaveDirectory") 	 = AddBS( JustPath( Thisform.pcArqEmail) )
*!*											.cOption("AutosaveFilename")  	 = JustFname( Thisform.pcArqEmail)
*!*											.cDefaultPrinter = "PDFCreator"
*!*											.cPrinterStop 	 = .F.
*!*										EndIf
*!*									EndWith

*!*									If llPDFStart = .T.	
*!*										For lnPDFCount = 1 To 200
*!*											If Thisform.oPdf.cDefaultPrinter = "PDFCreator"
*!*												Exit
*!*											EndIf
*!*											Sleep(500)	&& Sleep IN WIN32API
*!*										Next lnPDFCount

*!*										If Thisform.oPdf.cDefaultPrinter # "PDFCreator"
*!*											lPrintPDFCreator = .F.
*!*											MessageBox( "Problemas para criar a Default-Printer" +Chr(13) +;
*!*														"ErrorNr: " + Str( Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Number"), 3 ) +Chr(13) +;
*!*														"Descr: " 	+ Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Description"), 48, "AtenńŃo" )
*!*										EndIf
*!*									EndIf
*!*								EndIf

*!*								If lPrintPDFCreator = .T. And llPDFStart = .T.
*!*									ThisForm.Documento()				

*!*									Sleep( 500 )		&& Milliseconds

*!*									lnMaxSleep  = 0
*!*									nReadyState = 0		&& Esta var ķ usada dentro do -> PDF_Event()	&& C:\FrameWork\ReportPreview\PDF_Event.prg

*!*								lnErrorNr = Thisform.oPdf.cErrorDetail("Number")
*!*								lnErrorNr = Iif( Type( "lnErrorNr" )=="N", lnErrorNr, Val( TransForm( lnErrorNr ) ) )

*!*								Thisform.oPdf.cClose()
*!*								Thisform.oPdf = Null
*!*								Wait Clear
*!*							Else
*!*								If ThisForm.Registry1.IsKey([PDFCreatorBeta.JobQueue])
*!*									oPrint = CreateObject('PDFCreatorBeta.PdfCreatorobj')
*!*									If oprint.IsInstanceRunning
*!*										lPrintPDFCreator = .F.
*!*										MessageBox( [PDFCreator jß estß sendo executado.] +Chr(13) +;
*!*													[Feche e tente novamente.], 48, "AtenńŃo" )								
*!*									Else
*!*										oPrint = oPrint.GetPDFCreatorPrinters()
*!*										lcPDFPrinter = oPrint.GetPrinterByIndex(0) && Pega o nome da impressora PDFCreator
*!*										
*!*										Set Printer to name (lcPDFPrinter)
*!*										
*!*										Release oPrint								

*!*										Thisform.oPdf = CreateObject('PDFCreatorBeta.JobQueue')
*!*										
*!*										Wait Window Chr(13) + [Aguarde... Gerando o Arquivo PDF] + Chr(13) Nowait NoClear				

*!*										Thisform.oPdf.Initialize

*!*										ThisForm.Documento()				

*!*										if !Thisform.oPdf.WaitForJob(5)
*!*										Else
*!*											job = Thisform.oPdf.NextJob()
*!*											job.SetProfileSetting('OpenViewer','false') && ķ o responsßvel para escolher se o documento serß aberto ou nŃo ap¾s gravańŃo automßtica.
*!*											job.SetProfileSetting('AuthorTemplate','RODES') && Autor que gerou o PDF
*!*											job.SetProfileSetting('TitleTemplate','') && TĒtulo do PDF
*!*										*!*		job.SetProfileSetting('ShowProgress','false') && Se mostra a barra de progresso

*!*											job.ConvertTo(Thisform.pcArqEmail)

*!*											For lnPDFCount = 1 To 200
*!*												If job.IsFinished
*!*													Exit
*!*												EndIf
*!*												Sleep(500)	&& Sleep IN WIN32API
*!*											Next lnPDFCount

*!*											If !job.IsFinished Or !job.IsSuccessful	
*!*												lPrintPDFCreator = .F.
*!*										    Endif
*!*										Endif

*!*										Thisform.oPdf.ReleaseCom()
*!*										Set Printer to Name (lcDefaultPrinter)
*!*										CLEAR DLLS "Sleep"
*!*										Thisform.oPdf = Null
*!*										Wait Clear																			
*!*									Endif
*!*								Endif
*!*							Endif
					Endif

					If lPrintPDFCreator = .T.
						If Type([Thisform.oEMAIL]) = [O]
							If !File(Thisform.pcArqEmail)
*!*									MessageBox([Problemas na gerańŃo do arquivo ] + Thisform.pcArqEmail + [!], 48, [AtenńŃo])
								Return .f.
							EndIf						
							** Anexar o Arquivo no Email. Enviar o Email
							Wait Window Chr(13)+ [Aguarde... gerando EMAIL com o Arquivo] + Chr(13) + Thisform.oEMAIL.cAnexo + Chr(13) Nowait NoClear

												** As Propriedades do objeto oEMAIL, foram acrescentadas no form SigPrPdf
							If Thisform.mEmail( 	Thisform.oEMAIL.cFrom, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cTo, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cCC, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cAssunto, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cCorpo, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cAnexo, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cSmtpServer, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.nSmtpServerPort, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cSendUserName, ;
													Thisform.oEMAIL.cSendPassWord 	)
								Wait Clear
								MessageBox([Email enviado com sucesso.], 64, [Envio de Email])
								Thisform.oEMAIL = Null
							EndIf 						
						Else 
							If File(Thisform.pcArqEmail)
								MessageBox([Arquivo ] + Thisform.pcArqEmail + [ gerado com sucesso!],64,[Aviso])
							Else
*!*									MessageBox([Problemas na gerańŃo do arquivo ] + Thisform.pcArqEmail + [!], 48, [AtenńŃo])
								MessageBox([Relat¾rio nŃo estß preparado para gerar o arquivo ] + Thisform.pcArqEmail + [!], 48, [AtenńŃo])
							EndIf
						EndIf
					EndIf				
				Endif
		EndCase
	Else
		=Messagebox([NŃo Existe MovimentańŃo...],0+48, [GerańŃo de Relat¾rio])
	EndIf
Else
	=MessageBox([Falha Na ConexŃo! Favor Reinicializar o Processo!], 0+48, [Erro])
EndIf

Set Separator To (lcSep)
Set Point To (lcPnt)
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE maddcoluna
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE maddcoluna
Lparameters lcColCampo, lcColMascara, lcColTitulo, llIngrid, lcCtrlSource, llImage, llNoGrid
Local lcMcrCol1, lnNcolgrid, lnNctrlsource1

With This
	m.lcColMascara = Iif(Type('m.lcColMascara')=='C',m.lcColMascara,'')
	m.lcColTitulo = Iif(Type('m.lcColTitulo')=='C',m.lcColTitulo,'')
	m.llIngrid = Iif(Type('m.llIngrid')=='L',m.llIngrid,.f.)
	m.lcCtrlSource = Iif(Type('m.lcCtrlSource')=='C',m.lcCtrlSource,'')
	m.lcCtrlSource = Iif(Empty(m.lcCtrlSource),(.pcCursor+[.]+m.lcColCampo),m.lcCtrlSource)
	m.llImage = Iif(Type('m.llImage')=='L', m.llImage, .f.)
	m.llNoGrid = Iif(Type('m.llNoGrid')=='L', m.llNoGrid, .f.)
	m.lnNctrlsource1 = Iif(IsNull(.paCtrlSource1(1,1)),1,(Alen(.paCtrlSource1,1)+1))

	.pcCamposLista1 = (.pcCamposLista1+m.lcColCampo+',')

	If Not m.llNoGrid
		Declare .paCtrlSource1(m.lnNctrlsource1,1)

		.paCtrlSource1(m.lnNctrlsource1,1) = m.lcCtrlSource

		If m.llImage
			If Not Type('This.imgLista1')=='O'
				This.AddObject('imgLista1', 'Image')

				With This.imgLista1
					.Enabled = .t.
					.Visible = .f.
					.Width = 110
					.Height = 74
					.Stretch = 1
					.AddProperty('pcField1', m.lcCtrlSource)
					.AddProperty('pcFileImg1', (Addbs(Sys(2023)) + Sys(2015) + '.jpg'))
				EndWith 
			EndIf 
		Else 
			With .GridProc
				m.lnNcolgrid = (.ColumnCount+1)
				If m.lnNcolgrid==0
					m.lnNcolgrid = 1
				EndIf
				.AddColumn(m.lnNcolgrid)
				m.lcMcrCol1 = AllTrim(Str(.ColumnCount,20))
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..ControlSource = ''
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Width = 1
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Movable = .f.
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Resizable = .f.
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Format = 'K'
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..InputMask = m.lcColMascara
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..SelectOnEntry = .f.
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..FontName = 'Courier New'
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..FontSize = 9
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Alignment = 3
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.Caption =  AllTrim(m.lcColTitulo)
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.FontName = 'Arial'
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.FontSize = 8
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..Header1.Alignment = 2
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..AddObject("ingrid1","fwGrdLocate1",.t.)
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..CurrentControl = 'ingrid1'
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..RemoveObject("Text1")
				.Column&lcMcrCol1..ReadOnly = .T.
				With .Column&lcMcrCol1..ingrid1
					.Visible = .t.
					.Format = 'K'
					.InputMask = m.lcColMascara
					.FontName = 'Courier New'
					.FontSize = 9
					.Alignment = 3
					.BorderStyle = 0
					.Margin = 0
					.Height = 25
					.Width = 100
					.Tag = Transform(m.llIngrid,'@!')
					.ckeyfilter = ''
					.clocateexpression = ''
					.cordertag = ''
					.cprefixseek = ''
					.csearchstring = ''
					.cseektag = ''
					.lingridactive = .f.
					.nwaittime = (_DblClick)
				EndWith
			EndWith
		EndIf 
	EndIf 
EndWith

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mleituralista
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mleituralista
Local lnErro1,lcMcrSql1,lcCursor,lnCnt1mloObjgrid1,lcCampo1,lnWidthGrid1,leBusca1,lcStrWhere1,lcStrWhere2,lcMcrVar,lnCnt1

With This
	This.GridProc.RecordSource = ''
	m.lcCursor = .pcCursor
	m.leBusca1 = .peBusca
	m.leBusca2 = .peBusca
	If Type('m.leBusca2')=='C'
		m.leBusca2 = Alltrim(m.leBusca2)
	EndIf 
	m.lnErro1 = .pnIdConn1
	.pcCamposLista1 = Iif(Right(.pcCamposLista1,1)==',',Left(.pcCamposLista1,(Len(.pcCamposLista1)-1)),.pcCamposLista1)
	.pnTotalNreg1 = (.pnTotalNreg1+.pnNreg1)
	m.lcStrWhere1 = []

	If Not IsNull(This.paFiltro1(1,1))
		m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
		For m.lnCnt1=1 To ALen(This.paFiltro1,1)
			m.lcMcrVar = ('peconteudo'+AllTrim(Str(m.lnCnt1,20,0)))

			Private &lcMcrVar.

			&lcMcrVar. = This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,2)
			m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1+[ and ]+Lower(AllTrim(This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,1)))+[=?m.]+m.lcMcrVar)
		EndFor
	Else 
		If Not IsNull(This.pcFiltro1)
			m.lcStrWhere1 = ([ where ] + Alltrim(This.pcFiltro1))
		EndIf 
	EndIf
	If (goSistema.BuscaP Or .pnTotalNreg1 > 0) And Not This.plNaoFiltraCam1 && Tiago - 01/02/2016 - IncluĒdo checagem se ativou busca por like (BUSCAP) - .pnTotalNreg1>0 And Not This.plNaoFiltraCam1
		If !goSistema.BuscaP Or Type('m.leBusca1')=='N'
			If Empty(m.lcStrWhere1)
				m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
			EndIf
			Private pebusca1,pebusca2
			m.pebusca1 = m.leBusca1
			m.pebusca2 = Iif((Type('m.leBusca1')=='C'.And..Not.Empty(m.leBusca1)),PadR(AllTrim(m.leBusca1),Len(m.leBusca1),Chr(254)),m.leBusca1)
			m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1+;
			                Iif((Type('m.leBusca1')=='N'.And.m.leBusca1>0),;
			                    [ and ]+.pcCampo+[>=?m.pebusca1],;
			                    Iif((Type('m.leBusca1')=='C'.And..Not.Empty(m.leBusca1)),;
			                        [ and ]+.pcCampo+[ between ?m.pebusca1 and ?m.pebusca2],;
			                        [])))
		Else
			If Empty(m.lcStrWhere1)
				m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
			EndIf		
			m.lcStrWhere1 = m.lcStrWhere1 + [ And ] + .pcCampo + [ Like '%] + Alltrim(m.leBusca1) + [%']
		Endif
	EndIf
	m.lcMcrSql1 = ([select]+;
	               Iif(.pnTotalNreg1>0,[ top ]+AllTrim(Str(.pnTotalNreg1,20,0)),[])+;
	               [ ]+.pcCamposLista1+;
	               [ from ]+.pcTabela+;
	               m.lcStrWhere1+;
	               Iif(Empty(.pcOrdemCursor),[],[ order by ]+.pcOrdemCursor))
	If Used(m.lcCursor)
		Use In (m.lcCursor)
	EndIf

	If m.lnErro1>0
		m.lnErro1 = fSQLExec(This.pnIdConn1, m.lcMcrSql1, m.lcCursor, This.plCancel)
	EndIf

	If Not Used(m.lcCursor)
		m.lcMcrSql1 = [select ] + .pcCamposLista1 + [ from ] + .pcTabela + [ where 0=1]

		= SQLExec(This.pnIdConn1, m.lcMcrSql1, m.lcCursor)

	EndIf 

	If Used(m.lcCursor)
		Select (m.lcCursor)
		Set Order To ('') In (m.lcCursor)
		Locate For .f.

		With .GridProc
			.RecordSource = m.lcCursor
			m.lnCnt1 = 0
			m.lnWidthGrid1 = 0

			For Each m.loObjgrid1 In .Columns
				If Lower(m.loObjgrid1.BaseClass)=='column'
					m.lnCnt1 = (m.lnCnt1+1)
					m.lcCampo1 = (m.lcCursor+'.'+AllTrim(Field(m.lnCnt1,m.lcCursor)))
					m.loObjgrid1.ControlSource = This.paCtrlSource1(m.loObjgrid1.ColumnOrder,1)
					m.lcMcrKey1 = Lower(Alltrim(Field(m.lnCnt1,m.lcCursor)))
					m.lcMcrTag1 = Left(m.lcMcrKey1,10)
					Select (lcCursor)
					
					If (Not Type(m.lcCampo1)=='M' And (Not Type(m.lcMcrKey1)=='C' Or Len(&lcMcrKey1.)<=240))
						Index On &lcMcrKey1. Tag &lcMcrTag1.
					EndIf 
					If m.loObjgrid1.Width <= 14
						m.lnTamanho = (Iif(Len(m.loObjgrid1.InputMask)>2.Or..Not.InList(Type(m.lcCampo1),"C","D"),;
							               Len(m.loObjgrid1.InputMask),;
							               Iif(Type(m.lcCampo1)=="C",;
							                   Len(Evaluate(m.lcCampo1)),;
							                   10)))
						m.loObjgrid1.Width = (Int(m.lnTamanho*7)+10)
						m.loObjgrid1.InputMask = Iif((.Not.Type(m.lcCampo1)=='N'.Or.Left(m.loObjgrid1.InputMask,1)=='9'),m.loObjgrid1.InputMask,'')
						m.loObjgrid1.ingrid1.InputMask = m.loObjgrid1.InputMask
						m.lnWidthGrid1 = (m.lnWidthGrid1+m.loObjgrid1.Width)

					Else 

						m.lnWidthGrid1 = (m.lnWidthGrid1+m.loObjgrid1.Width)

					EndIf
					With m.loObjgrid1.ingrid1
						.cordertag = m.lcMcrTag1
						.cseektag  = m.lcMcrTag1
						.lingridactive = (Not Type(m.lcCampo1)=='M' And (Not Type(m.lcMcrKey1)=='C' Or Len(&lcMcrKey1.)<=240))
					EndWith
				EndIf
			EndFor
			If .Not.m.lnWidthGrid1==0
				.Width = Max((m.lnWidthGrid1+64),128)

			EndIf
			.Refresh

		EndWith

		.cmdGprocessa.cmdOk.Enabled = (Used(m.lcCursor).And.RecCount(m.lcCursor)>0.And.RecCount(m.lcCursor)>=.pnTotalNreg1)
		.cmdGprocessa.cmdOk.Cancel = (.cmdGprocessa.cmdOk.Enabled)

		Select (lcCursor)
		Set Order To ('') In (lcCursor)

		If Not Empty(.pcCampo)
			If Type(lcCursor+'.'+.pcCampo) == 'C'
				Locate For (Upper(Evaluate(lcCursor+'.'+.pcCampo)) = Upper(m.leBusca2))
			Else 
				Locate For (Evaluate(lcCursor+'.'+.pcCampo) >= m.leBusca2)
			
			EndIf 

		Else
			Locate For .f.

		EndIf

	Else
		= MessageBox('Falha na ConexŃo,'+Chr(13)+'Favor Reinicializar o Processo.',(0+48+0),'Erro na Procura')

	EndIf

EndWith

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE msaida
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE msaida

Local laCampos1(1,5)
Local lcCursor, lnErro1, lcCampoLista1, lcStrWhere1, lnNCampos1, lcMcrVar, lnErro1, lcMcrsql1

With This
	If Not .plChkSaida1
		If Type('This.imgLista1.pcFileImg1')=='C' And File(This.imgLista1.pcFileImg1)
			This.imgLista1.pcField1 = ''
			This.imgLista1.Picture = ''
			This.imgLista1.Visible = .f.

			Delete File (This.imgLista1.pcFileImg1)
		EndIf 

		m.lcCursor = .pcCursor
		m.leBusca = .peBusca
		m.lnErro1 = .pnIdConn1
		.pcCamposLista1 = Iif(Right(.pcCamposLista1,1)==',',Left(.pcCamposLista1,(Len(.pcCamposLista1)-1)),.pcCamposLista1)
		m.lcCampoLista1 = .pcCamposLista1
		m.lcStrWhere1 = []
		m.lcMcrVar = []

		If Used(m.lcCursor) 
			If Reccount(m.lcCursor) > 0 And Not Eof(m.lcCursor)
			
				If Not Empty(lcCampoLista1)
					Private &lcCampoLista1.
					
				EndIf 

				Select (m.lcCursor)
				Set Order To ('') In (m.lcCursor)
				Scatter Memo Memvar

				If Not IsNull(This.paFiltro1(1,1))
					m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
					For m.lnCnt1=1 To ALen(This.paFiltro1,1)
						m.lcMcrVar = ('peconteudo'+AllTrim(Str(m.lnCnt1,20,0)))

						Private &lcMcrVar.

						&lcMcrVar. = This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,2)
						m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1+[ and ]+Lower(AllTrim(This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,1)))+[=?m.]+m.lcMcrVar)
					EndFor
				Else 
					If Not IsNull(This.pcFiltro1)
						m.lcStrWhere1 = ([ where ] + Alltrim(This.pcFiltro1))
					EndIf 
				EndIf
				Declare m.laCampos1(1,5)
				m.laCampos1 = Null
				m.lnNCampos1 = AFields(m.laCampos1,m.lcCursor)
				
				If m.lnNCampos1>0
					If Empty(m.lcStrWhere1)
						m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
					EndIf
					For m.lnCnt1=1 To m.lnNCampos1
						If Not InList(Lower(m.laCampos1(m.lnCnt1,2)),'g','m')
							m.lcMcrVar = [m.]+Lower(AllTrim(m.laCampos1(m.lnCnt1,1)))
							If (InList(Lower(m.laCampos1(m.lnCnt1,2)),'d','t') And IsEmpty(&lcMcrVar.))
								&lcMcrVar. = Null
							EndIf 
							m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1+[ and ]+Lower(AllTrim(m.laCampos1(m.lnCnt1,1)))+[=?m.]+Lower(AllTrim(m.laCampos1(m.lnCnt1,1))))
						EndIf 
					EndFor 
				EndIf

			Else 
				m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=1]

			EndIf 
			m.lcMcrSql1 = ([select ]+ this.pcFields +;
			               [ from ]+.pcTabela+;
			               m.lcStrWhere1)
			If Used(m.lcCursor)
				Use In (m.lcCursor)
			EndIf
			If m.lnErro1>0
				m.lnErro1 = fSQLExec(This.pnIdConn1,m.lcMcrSql1,.pcCursor)
			EndIf
			If Used(m.lcCursor)
				Select (m.lcCursor)
				Set Order To ('') In (m.lcCursor)
				Locate
			Else 
				= MessageBox('Falha na ConexŃo,'+Chr(13)+'Favor Reinicializar o Processo.',(0+48+0),'Erro na Procura')
				.Release
			EndIf 
		Else
			= MessageBox('Falha na ConexŃo,'+Chr(13)+'Favor Reinicializar o Processo.',(0+48+0),'Erro na Procura')
			.Release
		EndIf
		.plChkSaida1 = .t.
	EndIf 
EndWith

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Destroy
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Destroy
goSistema.BuscaP = .F.
This.Release 

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Release
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Release

If Not This.pOpnRelease
	This.pOpnRelease = .t.
	
	If This.Visible
		This.mSaida

	EndIf 

	If This.pnArea1 > 0 And Used(This.pnArea1)
		Select (This.pnArea1)

	EndIf

	On Key Label Escape

	Release m.This

EndIf

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Show
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Show

LPARAMETERS nStyle
Local lnConta1, lnHeightForm1, lnHeightForm2, lnHeightForm3, lnCnt1, lnLeftIni1

m.lnHeightForm1 = 0
m.lnHeightForm2 = 0
m.lnHeightForm2 = 0

With This
	.LockScreen = .t.
	
	With .GridProc
		.ScrollBars = 2
		.ReadOnly = .t.
		.Enabled = .t.
		.Visible = .t.
		.AllowHeaderSizing = .f.
		.AllowRowSizing = .f.
		.DeleteMark = .f.
		.ScrollBars = 2
		.HeaderHeight = 16
		.RowHeight = 16
		.Height = 225
		.Left = 5
		*.Top = 5

		m.lnHeightForm1 = (m.lnHeightForm1 + .Top + .Height)
		.SetAll("Visible",.t.,"TextLista")
		.SetAll('DynamicBackColor','Iif(RecNo(This.RecordSource)==This.Parent.pnRecno1,RGB(0,255,255),RGB(255,255,255))','Column')
	EndWith

	.mLeituraLista()

	.Width = (.GridProc.Width+10)

	With .cmdGprocessa
		.cmdZoom.Enabled = .f.
		.cmdZoom.Visible = (Type('This.imgLista1')=='O')
		.cmdZoom.Cancel = .f.
		.cmdOk.Enabled = (This.pnTotalNreg1 > 0)
		.cmdOk.Visible = (This.pnTotalNreg1 > 0)
		.cmdOk.Cancel = .f.
		.Enabled = (.cmdZoom.Visible Or .cmdOk.Visible)
		.Visible = (.cmdZoom.Visible Or .cmdOk.Visible)
		
		If .Visible 
			m.lnLeftIni1 = 5
			For m.lnCnt1=1 To .ButtonCount
				If .Buttons(m.lnCnt1).Visible
				   .Buttons(m.lnCnt1).Left = m.lnLeftIni1
				   m.lnLeftIni1 = (m.lnLeftIni1+.Buttons(m.lnCnt1).Width)
				EndIf
			EndFor
			.AutoSize = .f.
			.Width = (m.lnLeftIni1+5)
		Else
			.Width = 138
 		EndIf 
		If This.pnTotalNreg1 > 0
			.Left = (This.Width-  .Width - 5)
			.Top = (m.lnHeightForm1 + 5)

			m.lnHeightForm1 = (m.lnHeightForm1 + 5 + .Height)
		EndIf
	EndWith
	If Type('This.imgLista1')=='O'
		This.imgLista1.Left = 5
		This.imgLista1.Top = (This.GridProc.Top + This.GridProc.Height + 5)

		m.lnHeightForm1 = (This.imgLista1.Top + This.imgLista1.Height + 5)
		This.cmdGprocessa.Top = (m.lnHeightForm1 - This.cmdGprocessa.Height - 5)
	EndIf 

	.Height = (m.lnHeightForm1 + 5)
	.AutoCenter = .t.
	.Refresh
	.LockScreen = .f.
EndWith

= DoDefault()

ENDPROC

PROCEDURE LostFocus

On Key Label Escape

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Init
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Init

LParameters pIdc, lcTabela, lcCursor, lcCampo, leBusca, lcTitulo, leNreg1, lcOrdem, laFiltro1, llNaoFiltraCam1, llCancel, lcFields
Local lcOnErroCmd1,llOnErro1,llColumOk1,lnErro1,lcStrWhere1,lcMcrSql1,lcMcrVar,lnCnt1

pIdc = Iif(Type([pIdc])=[N], pIdc, 0)
m.lcTabela = Iif(Type('m.lcTabela')=='C',m.lcTabela,'')
m.lcCursor = Iif(Type('m.lcCursor')=='C',m.lcCursor,'')
m.lcCampo = Iif(Type('m.lcCampo')=='C',m.lcCampo,'')
m.leBusca = Iif(InList(Type('m.leBusca'),'C','N'),m.leBusca,'')
m.lcTitulo = Iif(Type('m.lcTitulo')=='C',m.lcTitulo,'SeleńŃo')
m.leNreg1 = Iif(Type('m.leNreg1')=='L',Iif(m.leNreg1,0,1000),Iif(Type('m.leNreg1')=='N'.And.m.leNreg1>0,m.leNreg1,1000))
m.lcOrdem = Iif(Type('m.lcOrdem')=='C',m.lcOrdem,'')
m.lcOrdem = Iif(Empty(m.lcOrdem),m.lcCampo,m.lcOrdem)
m.llNaoFiltraCam1 = Iif(Type('m.llNaoFiltraCam1')=='L', m.llNaoFiltraCam1, .f.)
m.llCancel = Iif(Type('m.llCancel')=='L', llCancel, .f.)
m.lcOnErroCmd1 = On('Error')
m.llOnErro1 = .f.
m.lcFields = Lower(AllTrim(Iif(Type('m.lcFields')=='C',m.lcFields,'')))

Set Safety Off

On Error m.llOnErro1 = .t.
m.llColumOk1 = (ALen(m.laFiltro1,2)==2 And Type('m.laFiltro1(1,1)')=='C')
On Error &lcOnErroCmd1.
Declare This.paFiltro1(1,1),This.paCtrlSource1(1,1)

This.pOpnRelease = .f.
This.paFiltro1 = Null
This.pcFiltro1 = Null
This.paCtrlSource1 = Null
This.plNaoFiltraCam1 = .f.
This.plCancel = m.llCancel
This.oleImgZ1.Visible = .F.
this.pcFields = Null

If m.llColumOk1
	= Acopy(m.laFiltro1,This.paFiltro1)
	This.plNaoFiltraCam1 = (m.llNaoFiltraCam1 And Not IsNull(This.paFiltro1))

Else 
	This.pcFiltro1 = Iif(Type('m.laFiltro1')=='C' And Not Empty(m.laFiltro1), m.laFiltro1, Null)
	This.plNaoFiltraCam1 = (m.llNaoFiltraCam1 And Not IsNull(This.pcFiltro1))

EndIf
If (pIdc > 0 And Not Empty(m.lcTabela).And..Not.Empty(m.lcCursor))
	With This
		.pnIdConn1 = pIdc
		.pnArea1 = Select()
		.pcTabela = Lower(AllTrim(m.lcTabela))
		.pcCursor = Lower(AllTrim(m.lcCursor))
		.pcCampo = Lower(AllTrim(m.lcCampo))
		.peBusca = m.leBusca
		.pnNreg1 = m.leNreg1
		.pnTotalNreg1 = 0
		.pcOrdemCursor = Lower(AllTrim(m.lcOrdem))
		.pcCamposLista1 = ''
		.pnRecno1 = 0
		.pnRecno2 = 0
		.Caption = Proper(AllTrim(m.lcTitulo))
		.GridProc.ColumnCount = 0
		.ControlBox = .f.
		.WindowType = 1
		.plAchouRegistro = .f.
		.plChkSaida1 = .f.
		If Empty(m.lcFields)
			m.lcFields = [*]
		Endif
		this.pcFields = m.lcFields
		
		If (.Not.Empty(.pcCampo).And.;
			.Not.Empty(m.leBusca).And.;
			InList(Type('m.leBusca'),'N','C'))
			m.lnErro1 = .pnIdConn1
			m.lcStrWhere1 = [ where 0=0]
			m.lcStrWhere1 = m.lcStrWhere1+[ and ]+.pcCampo+[=?m.peconteudo0]
			
			If Not IsNull(This.paFiltro1(1,1))
				For m.lnCnt1=1 To ALen(This.paFiltro1,1)
					m.lcMcrVar = ('peconteudo'+AllTrim(Str(m.lnCnt1,20,0)))

					Private &lcMcrVar.

					&lcMcrVar. = This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,2)
					m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1+[ and ]+Lower(AllTrim(This.paFiltro1(m.lnCnt1,1)))+[=?m.]+m.lcMcrVar)
				EndFor
			Else 
				If Not IsNull(This.pcFiltro1)
					m.lcStrWhere1 = ([ where ] + Alltrim(This.pcFiltro1))
				EndIf 
			EndIf
			Private peconteudo0
			m.peconteudo0 = m.leBusca
			*m.lcStrWhere1 = (m.lcStrWhere1)
			m.lcMcrSql1 = [select ] + m.lcFields + [ from ] + .pcTabela +	m.lcStrWhere1
			If Used(.pcCursor)
				Use In (.pcCursor)
			EndIf
			If m.lnErro1>0
				m.lnErro1 = fSQLExec(This.pnIdConn1,m.lcMcrSql1,.pcCursor)
			EndIf
			If Used(.pcCursor)
				m.lcMcrLocate = (.pcCursor+[.]+.pcCampo)

				Select (.pcCursor)
				Set Order To ('') In (.pcCursor)
				Locate For (&lcMcrLocate.==m.leBusca)

				.plAchouRegistro = (.Not.Eof(.pcCursor).And.&lcMcrLocate.==m.leBusca)
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndWith
EndIf

ThisForm.cntSombra.lblSombra.Caption = ThisForm.Caption
ThisForm.cntSombra.lblTitulo.Caption = ThisForm.Caption

ENDPROC

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE Hide
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE Hide

Local lcMcrLocate

With This
	.mSaida

	If .pnArea1 > 0 And Used(.pnArea1)
		Select (.pnArea1)

	EndIf

EndWith

On Key Label Escape

ENDPROC

		NoDefault

	EndIf

------------------------------------------------------------
* PROCEDURE mobjenabled
------------------------------------------------------------
PROCEDURE mobjenabled
LParameters loRef, llChk

Local lnObj

If llChk
	For lnObj=1 To loRef.ControlCount
		If (Inlist(Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass), [TEXTBOX], [OPTIONGROUP], [CHECKBOX], [EDITBOX], [COMBOBOX], [LISTBOX]) And Not Empty(loRef.Controls(lnObj).ClassLibrary))
			If (Inlist(Thisform.pcEscolha, [CONSULTAR], [EXCLUIR]) Or (Thisform.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR] And Not loRef.Controls(lnObj).plProcurar))
				loRef.Controls(lnObj).Enabled = (Not Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass)= [OPTIONGROUP])

				If (Type([loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly])=[L])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly = (Not (ThisForm.pcEscolha = [PROCURAR] And Not loRef.Controls(lnObj).plProcurar))
				EndIf
				
				If Inlist(Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass), [TEXTBOX], [EDITBOX], [COMBOBOX], [LISTBOX])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).DisabledForeColor = loRef.Controls(lnObj).ForeColor
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).DisabledBackColor = loRef.Controls(lnObj).BackColor
				EndIf
				
				If (Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass)= [OPTIONGROUP])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).SetAll([Enabled], .t., [OptionButton])
				EndIf
			Else
				loRef.Controls(lnObj).Enabled = .t.
				If (Type([loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly])=[L])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).ReadOnly = .f.
				EndIf
				
				If (Upper(loRef.Controls(lnObj).BaseClass) = [OPTIONGROUP])
					loRef.Controls(lnObj).SetAll([Enabled], .t., [OptionButton])
				EndIf
			EndIf
		EndIf
	EndFor
EndIf
* Fim **************************************************************************************
ENDPROC
